# <a name="search-the-audit-log-in-the-security--compliance-center"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-103">在安全与合规中心搜索审核日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-103">Search the audit log in the Office 365 Security & Compliance Center</span></span>

## <a name="introduction"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-104">简介</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-104">Introduction</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-105">需要了解用户是否查看了特定文档或从其邮箱中清除了某项？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-105">Need to find if a user viewed a specific document or purged an item from their mailbox?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-106">如果是，你可以使用 Office 365 安全 &amp; 合规中心搜索统一的审核日志，以查看 Office 365 组织中的用户和管理员活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-106">If so, you can use the Office 365 Security &amp; Compliance Center to search the unified audit log to view user and administrator activity in your Office 365 organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-107">为什么是统一的审核日志？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-107">Why a unified audit log?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-108">因为你可以在 Office 365 中搜索以下类型的用户和管理员活动：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-108">Because you can search for the following types of user and admin activity in Office 365:</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-109">SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的用户活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-109">Deleting documents in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-110">Exchange Online 中的用户活动（Exchange 邮箱审核日志记录）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-110">User activity in Exchange Online (Exchange mailbox audit logging)</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-111">SharePoint Online 中的管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-111">Admin activity in SharePoint Online</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-112">Azure Active Directory 中的管理员活动（Office 365 的目录服务）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-112">Admin activity in Azure Active Directory (the directory service for Office 365)</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-113">Exchange Online 中的管理员活动（Exchange 管理员审核日志记录）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-113">Admin activity in Exchange Online (Exchange admin audit logging)</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-114">Sway 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-114">User and admin activity in Sway</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-115">安全与合规中心中的电子数据展示活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-115">eDiscovery activities in the security and compliance center</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-116">Power BI 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-116">User and admin activity in Power BI</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-117">Microsoft Teams 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-117">User and admin activity in Microsoft Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-118">Dynamics 365 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-118">User and admin activity in Dynamics 365</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-119">Yammer 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-119">User and admin activity in Yammer</span></span>
 
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-120">Microsoft Flow 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-120">User and admin activity in Microsoft Flow</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-121">Microsoft Stream 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-121">User and admin activity in Microsoft Stream</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-122">Microsoft 工作区分析中的分析员和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-122">Analyst and admin activity in Microsoft Workplace Analytics</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-123">Microsoft PowerApps 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-123">User and admin activity in Microsoft PowerApps</span></span>
    
   
## <a name="before-you-begin"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-124">开始之前</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-124">Before you begin</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-125">在开始搜索 Office 365 审核日志之前，请务必阅读以下各项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-125">Be sure to read the following items before you start searching the Office 365 audit log.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-126">你（或其他管理员）必须首先开启审核日志记录，然后才能开始搜索 Office 365 审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-126">You (or another admin) must first turn on audit logging before you can start searching the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-127">若要将其打开，请单击安全与合规中心中的“**审核日志搜索**”页面上的“**开始录制用户和管理活动**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-127">To turn it on, click **Start recording user and admin activity** on the **Audit log search** page in the Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-128">（如果未看到此链接，则已为你的组织开启审核。）打开后，将显示一条消息，称正在准备审核日志，你可以在准备完成后数小时内运行搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-128">(If you don't see this link, auditing has already been turned on for your organization.) After you turn it on, a message is displayed that says the audit log is being prepared and that you can run a search in a couple of hours after the preparation is complete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-129">只需执行一次此操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-129">You should only have to do this once.</span></span> 
    
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="3863b-130">默认正在启用审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-130">We're in the process of turning on auditing by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-131">在这之前，可以按上文所述启用审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-131">Until then, you can turn it on as previously described.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-132">必须分配有 Exchange Online 中的“仅供查看审核日志”或“审核日志”角色才能搜索 Office 365 审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-132">You have to be assigned the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role in Exchange Online to search the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-133">默认情况下，在 Exchange 管理中心中的“**权限**”页上将这些角色分配给“合规性管理”和“组织管理”角色组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-133">By default, these roles are assigned to the Compliance Management and Organization Management role groups on the **Permissions** page in the Exchange admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-134">请注意，Office 365 和 Microsoft 365 中的全局管理员将自动添加为 Exchange Online 的组织管理角色组成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-134">Note Global administrators in Office 365 and Microsoft 365 are automatically added as members of the Organization Management role group in Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-135">若要让用户能够使用最低权限级别搜索 Office 365 审核日志，可以在 Exchange Online 中创建自定义角色组，添加“仅供查看审核日志”或“审核日志”角色，然后将用户添加为新角色组的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-135">To give a user the ability to search the Office 365 audit log with the minimum level of privileges, you can create a custom role group in Exchange Online, add the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role, and then add the user as a member of the new role group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-136">有关详细信息，请参阅[在 Exchange Online 中管理角色组](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=730688)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-136">For more information, see [Manage role groups in Exchange Online](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=730688).</span></span>
    
    > [!IMPORTANT]
    > <span data-ttu-id="3863b-137">如果在安全与合规中心中的“**权限**”页上向用户分配“仅供查看审核日志”或“审核日志”角色，则他们将无法搜索 Office 365 审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-137">If you assign a user the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role on the **Permissions** page in the Security & Compliance Center, they won't be able to search the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-138">必须在 Exchange Online 中分配权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-138">You have to assign the permissions in Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-139">这是因为用于搜索审核日志的基础 cmdlet 是 Exchange Online cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-139">This is because the underlying cmdlet used to search the audit log is an ExchangeOnline cmdlet.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-140">当用户或管理员执行审核活动时，将生成审核记录并将其存储在组织的 Office 365 审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-140">When an audited activity is performed by a user or admin, an audit record is generated and stored in the Office 365 audit log for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-141">保留审核记录（并且可在审核日志中搜索）的时间长度取决于你的 Office 365 订阅，具体而言是分配给特定用户的许可证类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-141">The length of time that an audit record is retained (and searchable in the audit log) depends on your Office 365 subscription, and specifically the type of the license that is assigned to a specific user.</span></span>

     - <span data-ttu-id="3863b-142">**Office 365 E3：** 审核记录可保留 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-142">**Office 365 E3:** Audit records are retained for 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-143">这意味着你可以在审核日志中搜索过去 90 天内执行的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-143">That means you can search the audit log for activities that were performed within the last 90 days.</span></span>

     - <span data-ttu-id="3863b-144">**Office 365 E5：** 审核记录也可保留 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-144">**Office 365 E5:** Audit records are also retained for 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-145">对于 E5 用户以及具有 E3 许可证和 Office 365 高级合规版附加许可证的用户，最终可将审核记录保留一年。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-145">Retaining audit records for one year may eventually be available for E5 users and users with an E3 license and an Office 365 Advanced Compliance add-on license.</span></span>

        > [!NOTE]
        > <span data-ttu-id="3863b-146">对于 E5 组织（或对于具有高级合规版附加许可证的 E3 组织内的用户），针对审核记录的一年保留期的个人预览版计划已对新注册关闭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-146">The private preview program for the one-year retention period for audit records for E5 organizations (or for users in E3 organizations that have Advanced Compliance add-on licenses) is closed to new enrollment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-147">当公共预览版提供一年保留期或正式发布时，本文将更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-147">This article will be updated when the one-year retention period is available in public preview or released for general availability.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-148">如果希望为组织关闭 Office 365 中的审核日志搜索，可以在连接到 Exchange Online 组织的远程 PowerShell 中运行以下命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-148">If you want to turn off audit log search in Office 365 for your organization, you can run the following command in remote PowerShell connected to your Exchange Online organization:</span></span>
    
  ```
  Set-AdminAuditLogConfig -UnifiedAuditLogIngestionEnabled $false
  ```

    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-149">若要再次打开审核搜索，可在 Exchange Online PowerShell 中运行以下命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-149">To turn on audit search again, you can run the following command in Exchange Online PowerShell:</span></span>
    
  ```
  Set-AdminAuditLogConfig -UnifiedAuditLogIngestionEnabled $true
  ```

    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-150">有关详细信息，请参阅[关闭 Office 365 中的审核日志搜索](turn-audit-log-search-on-or-off.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-150">For more information, see [Turn off audit log search in Office 365](turn-audit-log-search-on-or-off.md).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-151">如前所述，用于搜索审核日志的基础 cmdlet 是 Exchange Online cmdlet，即 **Search-UnifiedAuditLog**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-151">As previously stated, the underlying cmdlet used to search the audit log is an Exchange Online cmdlet, which is **Search-UnifiedAuditLog**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-152">这意味着可使用此 cmdlet 搜索 Office 365 审核日志，而不是使用安全与合规中心中的“**审核日志搜索**”页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-152">That means you can use this cmdlet to search the Office 365 audit log instead of using the **Audit log search** page in the Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-153">必须在连接到 Exchange Online 组织的远程 PowerShell 中运行此 cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-153">You have to run this cmdlet in remote PowerShell connected to your Exchange Online organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-154">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Search-UnifiedAuditLog](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=834776)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-154">For more information, see:[](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=834776)</span></span> 

    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-155">有关将 **Search-UnifiedAuditLog** cmdlet 所返回的搜索结果导出到 CSV 文件的信息，请参阅[导出、配置和查看审核日志记录](export-view-audit-log-records.md#tips-for-exporting-and-viewing-the-audit-log)中的“有关导出和查看审核日志的提示”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-155">For information about exporting the search results returned by the **Search-UnifiedAuditLog** cmdlet to a CSV file, see the "Tips for exporting and viewing the audit log" section in [Export, configure, and view audit log records](export-view-audit-log-records.md#tips-for-exporting-and-viewing-the-audit-log).</span></span>  

- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-156">若想以编程方式从 Office 365 审核日志下载数据，建议使用 Office 365 管理活动 API，而不是使用 PowerShell 脚本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-156">If you want to programmatically download data from the Office 365 audit log, we recommend that you use the Office 365 Management Activity API instead of using a PowerShell script.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-157">Office 365 管理活动 API 是一项 REST Web 服务，可用于为组织制定操作、安全和合规性监视解决方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-157">The Office 365 Management Activity API is a REST web service that you can use to develop operations, security, and compliance monitoring solutions for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-158">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Office 365 管理活动 API 参考](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/office-365-management-activity-api-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-158">For the operations reference, see [Office 365 Management Activity API reference](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/office-365-management-activity-api-reference).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-159">发生事件后，最多需要 30 分钟到 24 小时就可搜索结果中显示相应的审核日志条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-159">It can take up to 30 minutes or up to 24 hours after an event occurs for the corresponding audit log entry to be displayed in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-160">下表显示了 Office 365 中不同服务所花费的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-160">The following table shows the time it takes for the different services in Office 365.</span></span>
    
    |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-161">**Office 365 服务**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-161">**Office 365 service**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-162">**30 分钟**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-162">**30 minutes**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-163">**24 小时**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-163">**24 hours**</span></span>|
    |:-----|:-----|:-----|
    |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-164">高级威胁防护和威胁智能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-164">Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection and Threat Intelligence schema</span></span>  <br/> |![复选标记](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)| |

    |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-182">Microsoft Stream</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-182">Microsoft Stream</span></span>  <br/> |![复选标记](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/>| |
    |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-184">Microsoft Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-184">Microsoft Teams</span></span>  <br/> |![复选标记](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/> ||
    |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-186">Power BI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-186">Power BI</span></span>  <br/> |![复选标记](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/>| |
    |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-188">安全与合规中心</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-188">Security & Compliance Center</span></span>  <br/> |![复选标记](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/> ||
    |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-190">SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-190">SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business</span></span>  <br/> |![复选标记](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/> ||

- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-198">Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) 是 Office 365 的目录服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-198">Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) is the directory service for Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-199">统一审核日志包含用户、组、应用程序、域以及在 Microsoft 365 管理中心或 Azure 管理门户中执行的目录活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-199">The unified audit log contains user, group, application, domain, and directory activities performed in the Microsoft 365 admin center or in the Azure management portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-200">有关 Azure AD 事件的完整列表，请参阅 [Azure Active Directory 审核报告事件](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=616549)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-200">For a complete list of Azure AD events, see [Azure Active Directory Audit Report Events](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=616549).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-201">默认情况下，Power BI 的审核日志记录未启用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-201">Audit logging for Power BI isn't enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-202">若要在 Office 365 审核日志中搜索 Power BI 活动，必须在 Power BI 管理门户中启用审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-202">To search for Power BI activities in the Office 365 audit log, you have to enable auditing in the Power BI admin portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-203">有关说明，请参阅 [Power BI 管理门户](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs)中的“审核日志”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-203">For instructions, see the "Audit logs" section in [Power BI admin portal](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs).</span></span>
    
    
## <a name="search-the-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-204">搜索审核日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-204">Search the audit log</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-205">下面介绍在 Office 365 中搜索审核日志的流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-205">Here's the process for searching the audit log in Office 365.</span></span>
  
[<span data-ttu-id="3863b-206">步骤 1：运行审核日志搜索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-206">Step 1: Run an audit log search</span></span>](#step-1-run-an-audit-log-search)
  
[<span data-ttu-id="3863b-207">步骤 2：查看搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-207">Step 2: Download the search results</span></span>](#step-2-view-the-search-results)

[<span data-ttu-id="3863b-208">步骤 3：筛选搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-208">Step 3: Filter the search results</span></span>](#step-3-filter-the-search-results)

[<span data-ttu-id="3863b-209">步骤 4：将搜索结果导出到文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-209">Step 4: Export the search results to a file</span></span>](#step-4-export-the-search-results-to-a-file)



  
### <a name="step-1-run-an-audit-log-search"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-210">步骤 1：运行审核日志搜索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-210">Step 1: Run an audit log search</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="3863b-211">转到 [https://protection.office.com](https://protection.office.com)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-211">Go to [https://protection.office.com](https://protection.office.com).</span></span>
    
    > [!TIP]
    > <span data-ttu-id="3863b-212">使用专用浏览会话（而不是常规会话）来访问安全与合规中心，因为它会阻止你使用当前登录时使用的凭据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-212">Use a private browsing session (not a regular session) to access the Security & Compliance Center because this will prevent the credential that you are currently logged on with from being used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-213">若要在 Internet Explorer 或 Microsoft Edge 中打开 InPrivate 浏览会话，只需按 CTRL+SHIFT+P。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-213">To open an InPrivate Browsing session in Internet Explorer or Microsoft Edge, just press CTRL+SHIFT+P.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-214">若要在 Google Chrome（称为隐身窗口）中打开专用浏览会话，请按 CTRL+SHIFT+N。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-214">To open a private browsing session in Google Chrome (called an incognito window), press CTRL+SHIFT+N.</span></span> 
  
2. <span data-ttu-id="3863b-215">使用工作或学校帐户登录到 Office 365。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-215">Sign in to Office 365 using your work or school account.</span></span>
    
3. <span data-ttu-id="3863b-216">在安全与合规中心的左侧窗格中，单击“**搜索**”，然后单击“**审核日志搜索**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-216">In the left pane of the Security & Compliance Center, click **Search**, and then click **Audit log search**.</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-217">此时将显示“**审核日志搜索**”页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-217">The **New search** page is displayed.</span></span> 
    
    ![配置条件，然后单击“搜索”以运行报告](media/8639d09c-2843-44e4-8b4b-9f45974ff7f1.png)
  
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="3863b-219">必须首先打开审核日志记录，然后才能运行审核日志搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-219">You have to first turn on audit logging before you can run an audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-220">如果显示“**开始记录用户和管理员活动**”链接，请单击该链接以打开审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-220">If the **Start recording user and admin activity** link is displayed, click it to turn on auditing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-221">如果未看到此链接，则已为你的组织开启审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-221">If you don't see this link, auditing has already been turned on for your organization.</span></span> 
  
4. <span data-ttu-id="3863b-222">配置以下搜索条件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-222">Configure the following search criteria:</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-223">a.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-223">a.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-224">“**活动**”单击下拉列表以显示你可以搜索的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-224">**Activities** Click the drop-down list to display the activities that you can search for.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-225">已将用户和管理员活动整理到相关活动组中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-225">User and admin activities are organized in to groups of related activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-226">你可以选择特定活动，或单击活动组名称以选择该组中的所有活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-226">You can select specific activities or you can click the activity group name to select all activities in the group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-227">你也可以单击已选活动以取消选择。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-227">You can also click a selected activity to clear the selection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-228">运行搜索后，仅将显示所选活动的审核日志项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-228">After you run the search, only the audit log entries for the selected activities are displayed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-229">选择“**显示所有活动的结果**”将显示由所选用户或用户组执行的所有活动的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-229">Selecting **Show results for all activities** displays results for all activities performed by the selected user or group of users.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-230">Office 365 审核日志中记录了超过 100 个用户和管理员活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-230">Over 100 user and admin activities are logged in the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-231">单击本文主题处的“**已审核的活动**”选项卡可查看每个不同 Office 365 服务中每个活动的描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-231">Click the **Audited activities** tab at the topic of this article to see the descriptions of every activity in each of the different Office 365 services.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-232">b.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-232">b.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-233">“**开始日期**”和“**结束日期**”默认选择了过去七天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-233">**Start date** and **End date** The last seven days are selected by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-234">选择日期和时间范围，以显示在这段时间内发生的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-234">Select a date and time range to display the events that occurred within that period.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-235">日期和时间将以协调世界时 (UTC) 格式显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-235">The date and time are stored in Coordinated Universal Time (UTC) format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-236">可指定的最大日期范围为 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-236">The maximum date range that you can specify is 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-237">如果所选日期范围超过 90 天，将显示错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-237">An error is displayed if the selected date range is greater than 90 days.</span></span> 
    
    > [!TIP]
    > <span data-ttu-id="3863b-238">如果要使用为期 90 天的最大日期范围，请选择当前时间作为“**开始日期**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-238">If you're using the maximum date range of 90 days, select the current time for the **Start date**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-239">否则，你将收到说明开始日期早于结束日期的错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-239">Otherwise, you'll receive an error saying that the start date is earlier than the end date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-240">如果你在过去 90 天内打开了审核，则最大日期范围不能从打开审核的日期之前开始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-240">If you've turned on auditing within the last 90 days, the maximum date range can't start before the date that auditing was turned on.</span></span> 
  
    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-241">c.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-241">c.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-242">“**用户**”单击此框，然后选择要为其显示搜索结果的一名或多名用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-242">**Users** Click in this box and then select one or more users to display search results for.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-243">由你在此框中所选用户执行的所选活动的审核日志项目将显示在结果列表中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-243">The audit log entries for the selected activity performed by the users you select in this box are displayed in the list of results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-244">将此框留空以返回组织中所有用户（和服务帐户）的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-244">Leave this box blank to return entries for all users (and service accounts) in your organization.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-245">d.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-245">d.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-246">“**文件、文件夹或网站**”键入部分或完整的文件或文件夹名称，搜索与包含指定关键字的文件夹文件相关的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-246">**File, folder, or site** Type some or all of a file or folder name to search for activity related to the file of folder that contains the specified keyword.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-247">你还可以指定文件或文件夹的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-247">You can also specify a URL of a file or folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-248">如果使用 URL，请确保输入完整的 URL 路径，或者如果输入部分 URL，则请勿包含任何特殊字符或空格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-248">If you use a URL, be sure the type the full URL path or if you type a portion of the URL, don't include any special characters or spaces.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-249">将此框留空以返回组织中所有文件和文件夹的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-249">Leave this box blank to return entries for all files and folders in your organization.</span></span>
    
   <span data-ttu-id="3863b-250">**提示**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-250">**Tips**</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="3863b-251">如果要查找与**网站**相关的所有活动，请在 URL 后面添加通配符 (\*) 以返回该网站的所有条目，例如，**"https://contoso-my.sharepoint.com/personal/\*"**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-251">If you're looking for all activities related to a **site**, add the wildcard symbol (\*) after the URL to return all entries for that site; for example, **"https://contoso-my.sharepoint.com/personal/\*"**.</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="3863b-252">如果要查找与**文件**相关的所有活动，请在文件名后面添加通配符 (\*) 以返回该文件的所有条目，例如，**"\*Customer_Profitability_Sample.csv"**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-252">If you're looking for all activities related to a **file**, add the wildcard symbol (\*) before the file name to return all entries for that file; for example, **"\*Customer_Profitability_Sample.csv"**.</span></span>
    

    
5. <span data-ttu-id="3863b-253">单击“**搜索**”以使用搜索条件运行搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-253">Click **Search** to run the search using your search criteria.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-254">此时将加载搜索结果，片刻后将显示在“**结果**”下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-254">The search results are loaded, and after a few moments they are displayed under **Results**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-255">完成搜索后会显示找到的结果数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-255">When the search is finished, the number of results found is displayed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-256">“**结果**”窗格中最多可显示 5,000 个事件（每次加载 150 个）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-256">A maximum of 5,000 events will be displayed in the **Results** pane in increments of 150 events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-257">如果超过 5,000 个事件满足搜索条件，则将显示最近的 5,000 个事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-257">If more than 5,000 events meet the search criteria, the most recent 5,000 events are displayed.</span></span> 
    
    ![完成搜索后会显示结果数。](media/986216f1-ca2f-4747-9480-e232b5bf094c.png)
  
  
#### <a name="tips-for-searching-the-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-259">有关搜索审核日志的提示</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-259">Tips for searching the audit log</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-260">可以通过单击活动名称选择要搜索的特定活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-260">You can select specific activities to search for by clicking the activity name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-261">或者可以通过单击组名搜索该组中的所有活动（例如“**文件和文件夹活动**”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-261">Or you can search for all activities in a group (such as **File and folder activities**) by clicking the group name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-262">如果选择了活动，可以单击该活动以取消选择。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-262">If an activity is selected, you can click it to cancel the selection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-263">还可以使用搜索框显示包含所键入关键字的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-263">You can also use the search box to display the activities that contain the keyword that you type.</span></span>
    
    ![单击活动组名称以选择所有活动](media/3cde97cb-6f35-47c0-8612-ecd9c6ac36a3.png)
  
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-265">必须选择“**活动**”列表中的“**显示所有活动的结果**”才能显示 Exchange 管理员审核日志中的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-265">You have to select **Show results for all activities** in the **Activities** list to display events from the Exchange admin audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-266">此审核日志中的事件将在结果的“**活动**”列中显示 cmdlet 名称（例如 **Set-Mailbox**）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-266">Events from this audit log display a cmdlet name (for example, **Set-Mailbox**) in the **Activity** column in the results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-267">有关详细信息，请单击本主题中的“**已审核的活动**”选项卡，然后单击“**Exchange 管理员活动**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-267">For more information, click the **Audited activities** tab in this topic and then click **Exchange admin activities**.</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-268">同样，某些审核活动在“**活动**”列表中没有相应项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-268">Similarly, there are some auditing activities that don't have a corresponding item in the **Activities** list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-269">如果已知这些活动的操作名称，可搜索所有活动，然后通过在“**活动**”列对应的框中键入操作名称来筛选结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-269">If you know the name of the operation for these activities, you can search for all activities, then filter the results by typing the name of the operation in the box for the **Activity** column.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-270">有关筛选结果的详细信息，请参阅[步骤 3：筛选搜索结果](#step-3-filter-the-search-results)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-270">See [Step 3: Filter the search results](#step-3-filter-the-search-results) for more information about filtering the results.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-271">单击“**清除**”以清除当前搜索条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-271">Click **Clear** to clear the current search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-272">日期范围返回到默认值（过去七天）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-272">The date range returns to the default of the last seven days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-273">还可以单击“**全部清除以显示所有活动的结果**”以取消所有选定活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-273">You can also click **Clear all to show results for all activities** to cancel all selected activities.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-274">如果找到了 5,000 条结果，则可以假定可能存在超过 5,000 个符合搜索条件的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-274">If 5,000 results are found, you can probably assume that there are more than 5,000 events that met the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-275">你可以优化搜索条件并重新运行搜索以返回较少结果，也可以通过选择“**导出结果**”\>“**下载所有结果**”导出所有搜索结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-275">You can either refine the search criteria and rerun the search to return fewer results, or you can export all of the search results by selecting **Export results** \> **Download all results**.</span></span>

  
### <a name="step-2-view-the-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-276">步骤 2：查看搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-276">Step 2: Download the search results</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-277">审核日志搜索结果会显示在“**审核日志搜索**”页中的“**结果**”下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-277">The results of an audit log search are displayed under **Results** on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-278">如上文所述，最多显示 5,000 个最新事件（每次加载 150 个）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-278">As previously stated a maximum of 5,000 (newest) events are displayed in increments of 150 events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-279">若要显示更多事件，可以使用“**结果**”窗格中的滚动条，或按 **Shift+End** 显示随后的 150 个事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-279">To display more events you can use the scroll bar in the **Results** pane or you can press **Shift + End** to display the next 150 events.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-280">结果包含有关搜索返回的每个事件的以下信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-280">The results contain the following information about each event returned by the search.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-281">**日期：** 事件发生的日期和时间（采用 UTC 格式）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-281">**Date:** The date and time (in UTC format) when the event occurred.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-282">**IP 地址：** 记录活动时所用设备的 IP 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-282">The IP address of the device that was used when the activity was logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-283">IP 地址显示为 IPv4 或 IPv6 地址格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-283">The IP address is displayed in either an IPv4 or IPv6 address format.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-284">**用户：** 执行触发事件的操作的用户（或服务帐户）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-284">**User:** The user (or service account) who performed the action that triggered the event.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-285">**活动：** 用户执行的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-285">**Activity:** The activity performed by the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-286">此值对应于你在“**活动**”下拉列表中选定的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-286">This value corresponds to the activities that you selected in the **Activities** drop down list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-287">对于来自 Exchange 管理员审核日志的事件，此列中的值为 Exchange cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-287">For an event from the Exchange admin audit log, the value in this column is an Exchange cmdlet.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-288">**项目：** 由于相应活动而创建或修改的对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-288">**Item:** The object that was created or modified as a result of the corresponding activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-289">例如已查看或修改的文件或已更新的用户帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-289">For example, the file that was viewed or modified or the user account that was updated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-290">并非所有活动在此列中都具有值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-290">Not all activities have a value in this column.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-291">**详细信息：** 有关活动的其他详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-291">**Detail:** Additional information about an activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-292">同样，并非所有活动均具有值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-292">Again, not all activities have a value.</span></span> 
    
> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-293">单击“**结果**”下的列标题对结果进行排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-293">Click a column header under **Results** to sort the results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-294">你可以将结果按从 A 到 Z 或从 Z 到 A 的顺序排序。单击“**日期**”标题以将结果按从旧到新或从新到旧的顺序排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-294">You can sort the results from A to Z or Z to A. Click the **Date** header to sort the results from oldest to newest or newest to oldest.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="view-the-details-for-a-specific-event"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-295">查看特定事件的详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-295">View the details for a specific event</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-296">可以通过单击搜索结果列表中的事件记录查看有关事件的更多详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-296">You can view more details about an event by clicking the event record in the list of search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-297">此时将显示包含事件记录的详细属性的“**详细信息**”页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-297">A **Details** page is displayed that contains the detailed properties from the event record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-298">显示的属性取决于事件发生于的 Office 365 服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-298">The properties that are displayed depend on the Office 365 service in which the event occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-299">若要显示这些详细信息，请单击“**更多信息**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-299">To display these details, click **More information**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-300">有关说明，请参阅 [Office 365 审核日志中的属性详细信息](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-300">[Detailed properties in the Office 365 audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)</span></span>
  
![单击“详细信息”，查看审核日志事件记录的详细属性](media/6df582ae-d339-4735-b1a6-80914fb77a08.png)

  
### <a name="step-3-filter-the-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-302">步骤 3：筛选搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-302">Step 3: Filter the search results</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-303">除排序外，你还可以筛选审核日志搜索的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-303">In addition to sorting, you can also filter the results of an audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-304">这是一项可帮助你快速筛选特定用户或活动的结果的强大功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-304">This is a great feature that can help you quickly filter the results for a specific user or activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-305">你可以首先创建一个广泛的搜索范围，然后快速筛选结果以查看特定事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-305">You can initially create a wide search and then quickly filter the results to see specific events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-306">然后可以缩小搜索条件范围并重新运行搜索以返回更小、更简洁的结果集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-306">Then you can narrow the search criteria and rerun the search to return a smaller, more concise set of results.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-307">若要筛选结果，请执行以下操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-307">To filter the results:</span></span>
  
1. <span data-ttu-id="3863b-308">运行审核日志搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-308">Run an audit log search.</span></span>
    
2. <span data-ttu-id="3863b-309">结果显示后，单击“**筛选结果**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-309">When the results are displayed, click **Filter results**.</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-310">每个列标题下将显示关键字框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-310">Keyword boxes are displayed under each column header.</span></span>
    
3. <span data-ttu-id="3863b-311">根据要筛选的列，单击列标题下的其中一个框并键入字词。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-311">Click one of the boxes under a column header and type a word or phrase, depending on the column you're filtering on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-312">结果将动态重新调整以显示符合筛选条件的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-312">The results will dynamically readjust to display the events that match your filter.</span></span>
    
    ![在筛选器中键入一个单词，以显示匹配筛选的事件](media/542dc323-a997-402c-934b-cc5e218e50bc.png)
  
4. <span data-ttu-id="3863b-314">若要清除筛选器，请单击筛选器框中的“**X**”，或单击“**隐藏筛选**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-314">To clear a filter, click the **X** in the filter box or click **Hide filtering**.</span></span>
    
> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-315">若要显示 Exchange 管理员审核日志中的事件，请在“**活动**”筛选器框中键入 **-**（破折号）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-315">To display events from the Exchange admin audit log, type a **-** (dash) in the **Activity** filter box.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-316">这将在 Exchange 管理员事件的“**活动**”列中显示 cmdlet 名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-316">This will display cmdlet names, which are displayed in the **Activity** column for Exchange admin events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-317">然后你便可按字母顺序对 cmdlet 名称进行排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-317">Then you can sort the cmdlet names in alphabetical order.</span></span> 

### <a name="step-4-export-the-search-results-to-a-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-318">步骤 4：将搜索结果导出到文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-318">Step 4: Export the search results to a file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-319">可以将审核日志搜索的结果导出到本地计算机上的逗号分隔值 (CSV) 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-319">You can export the results of an audit log search to a comma-separated value (CSV) file on your local computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-320">可以在 Microsoft Excel 中打开此文件，然后使用搜索、排序、筛选和将（包含多个属性的）单列拆分为多列等功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-320">You can open this file in Microsoft Excel and use features such as search, sorting, filtering, and splitting a single column (that contains multiple properties) into multiple columns.</span></span>
  
1. <span data-ttu-id="3863b-321">运行审核日志搜索，然后修订搜索条件直到获得所需结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-321">Run an audit log search, and then revise the search criteria until you have the desired results.</span></span>
    
2. <span data-ttu-id="3863b-322">单击“**导出结果**”，然后选择下列选项之一：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-322">Click **Export results** and select one of the following options:</span></span> 
    
     - <span data-ttu-id="3863b-323">“**保存加载的结果”**：选择此选项可仅导出“**审核日志搜索**”页上“**结果**”之下显示的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-323">**Save loaded results:** Choose this option to export only the entries that are displayed under **Results** on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-324">下载的 CSV 文件包含（“日期”、“用户”、“活动”、“项目”和“详细信息”）页面上显示的相同列（和数据）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-324">The CSV file that is downloaded contains the same columns (and data) displayed on the page (Date, User, Activity, Item, and Details).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-325">包含审核日志项目中更多信息的 CSV 文件包括一额外列（名为“**更多**”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-325">An extra column (named **More**) is included in the CSV file that contains more information from the audit log entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-326">由于你将导出“**审核日志搜索**”页上已加载（且可查看）的相同结果，因此最多可导出 5,000 个条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-326">Because you're exporting the same results that are loaded (and viewable) on the **Audit log search** page, a maximum of 5,000 entries are exported.</span></span> 
    
     - <span data-ttu-id="3863b-327">“**下载所有结果**”：选择此选项以导出符合搜索条件的 Office 365 审核日志中的所有条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-327">**Download all results:** Choose this option to export all entries from the Office 365 audit log that meet the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-328">对于较大的搜索结果集，选择此选项可下载审核日志的所有条目以及可在“**审核日志搜索**”页上显示的 5,000 条审核记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-328">For a large set of search results, choose this option to download all entries from the audit log in addition to the 5,000 audit records that can be displayed on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-329">此选项会将原始数据从审核日志下载到 CSV 文件，并在名为“**AuditData**”的列中包含审核日志项目中的其他信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-329">This option downloads the raw data from the audit log to a CSV file, and contains additional information from the audit log entry in a column named **AuditData**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-330">如果选择此导出选项，下载该文件可能需要更长时间，因为文件可能比选择其他选项下载的文件大得多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-330">It may take longer to download the file if you choose this export option because the file may be much larger than the one that's downloaded if you choose the other option.</span></span>
    
       > [!IMPORTANT]
       > <span data-ttu-id="3863b-331">你可以将最多 50,000 个条目从单个审核日志搜索中下载到 CSV 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-331">You can download a maximum of 50,000 entries to a CSV file from a single audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-332">如果下载了 50,000 个条目到 CSV 文件，则可以假定可能存在超过 50,000 个符合搜索条件的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-332">If 50,000 entries are downloaded to the CSV file, you can probably assume there are more than 50,000 events that met the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-333">若要导出的条目超出此限制，请尝试使用日期范围以减少审核日志项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-333">To export more than this limit, try using a date range to reduce the number of audit log entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-334">你可能需要使用更小日期范围运行多个搜索来导出超过 50,000 个条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-334">You might have to run multiple searches with smaller date ranges to export more than 50,000 entries.</span></span> 
  
3. <span data-ttu-id="3863b-335">选择导出选项后，窗口底部将显示一条消息，提示你打开 CSV 文件并将其保存到“下载”文件夹或特定文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-335">After you select an export option, a message is displayed at the bottom of the window that prompts you to open the CSV file, save it to the Downloads folder, or save it to a specific folder.</span></span>
 
#### <a name="more-information-about-exporting-and-viewing-audit-log-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-336">有关导出和查看审核日志搜索结果的详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-336">More information about exporting and viewing audit log search results</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-337">如果下载所有搜索结果，则 CSV 文件将包含一个名为“**AuditData**”的列，其中包含每个事件的其他信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-337">If you download all search results, the CSV file contains a column named **AuditData**, which contains additional information about each event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-338">此列中的数据由一个 JSON 对象组成，其中包含审核日志记录中的多个属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-338">The data in this column consists of a JSON object that contains multiple properties from the audit log record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-339">JSON 对象中的每个 *property:value* 对均由逗号分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-339">Each *property:value* pair in the JSON object is separated by a comma.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-340">你可以使用 Excel 中的 Power Query 编辑器的 JSON 转换工具将“**AuditData**”列拆分为多个列，以使 JSON 对象中的每个属性具有自己的列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-340">You can use the JSON transform tool in the Power Query Editor in Excel to split **AuditData** column into multiple columns so that each property in the JSON object has its own column.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-341">这让你能够对一个或多个属性进行排序和筛选。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-341">This lets you sort and filter on one or more of these properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-342">有关使用 Power Query 编辑器转换 JSON 对象的分步说明，请参阅[导出、配置和查看审核日志记录](export-view-audit-log-records.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-342">For step-by-step instructions using the Power Query Editor to transform the JSON object, see [Export, configure, and view audit log records](export-view-audit-log-records.md).</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-343">拆分“**AuditData**”列后，你可以对“**操作**”列进行筛选以显示特定类型活动的详细属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-343">After you split the **AuditData** column, you can filter on the **Operations** column to display the detailed properties for a specific type of activity.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-344">“**下载所有结果**”选项可将原始数据从 Office 365 审核日志下载到 CSV 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-344">The **Download all results** option downloads the raw data from the Office 365 audit log to a CSV file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-345">此文件包含的列名（“CreationDate”、“UserIds”、“操作”、“AuditData”）与选择“**保存已加载结果**”选项时下载的文件列名不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-345">This file contains different column names (CreationDate, UserIds, Operation, AuditData) than the file that's downloaded if you select the **Save loaded results** option.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-346">对于同一活动，两个不同 CSV 文件中的值可能也有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-346">The values in the two different CSV files for the same activity may also be different.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-347">例如，CSV 文件的“**操作**”列中的活动值可能与显示在“**审核日志搜索**”页上的“**活动**”列中的“用户友好”名称不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-347">For example, the activity in the **Action** column in the CSV file and may have a different value than the "user-friendly" name that's displayed in the **Activity** column on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-348">例如，分别为“MailboxLogin”与“用户已登录到邮箱”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-348">For example, MailboxLogin vs. User signed in to mailbox.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-349">下载（包含来自不同 Office 365 服务的事件的）搜索查询的所有结果时，CSV 文件中的“**AuditData**”列将含有不同属性，具体取决于在哪种服务中执行操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-349">When you download all results from a search query that contains events from different Office 365 services, the **AuditData** column in the CSV file contains different properties depending on which service the action was performed in.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-350">例如，来自 Exchange 和 Azure AD 审核日志的条目包含一个名为 **ResultStatus** 的属性，它指示操作是否成功。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-350">For example, entries from Exchange and Azure AD audit logs include a property named **ResultStatus** that indicates if the action was successful or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-351">来自 SharePoint 的事件不包含此属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-351">This property isn't included for events in SharePoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-352">类似地，SharePoint 事件具有用于标识文件和文件夹相关活动的网站 URL 的属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-352">Similarly, SharePoint events have a property that identifies the site URL for file and folder-related activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-353">若要缓和此行为，建议使用多个搜索导出单个服务中活动的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-353">To mitigate this behavior, consider using different searches to export the results for activities from a single service.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="3863b-354">有关下载所有结果时 CSV 文件的“**AuditData**”列中所列各个属性的说明以及每个属性适用的服务，请参阅 [Office 365 审核日志中的属性详细信息](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-354">For a description of many of the properties that are listed in the **AuditData** column in the CSV file when you download all results, and the service each one applies to, see [Detailed properties in the Office 365 audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md).</span></span>

## <a name="audited-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-355">已审核的活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-355">Audited activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-356">本节中的表介绍了 Office 365 中经审核的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-356">The tables in this section describe the activities that are audited in Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-357">你可以通过在安全与合规中心中搜索审核日志来搜索这些事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-357">You can search for these events by searching the audit log in the security and compliance center.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-358">这些表对相关活动或特定 Office 365 服务中的活动进行分组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-358">These tables group related activities or the activities from a specific Office 365 service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-359">表中包含显示在“**活动**”下拉列表中的友好名称以及导出搜索结果时显示在审核记录详细信息和 CSV 文件中的相应操作的名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-359">The tables include the friendly name that's displayed in the **Activities** drop-down list and the name of the corresponding operation that appears in the detailed information of an audit record and in the CSV file when you export the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-360">有关详细信息的说明，请参阅 [Office 365 审核日志中的属性详细信息](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-360">For descriptions of the detailed information, see [Detailed properties in the Office 365 audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md).</span></span>

### <a name="file-and-page-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-386">文件和页面活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-386">File and page activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-387">下表介绍了 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的文件和页面活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-387">The following table describes the file and page activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span>
  
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-388">**友好名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-388">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-389">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-389">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-390">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-390">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-391">已访问文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-391">Accessed a file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-392">FileAccessed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-392">FileAccessed</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-393">用户或系统帐户访问文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-393">User or system account accesses a file.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-394">(无)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-394">(none)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-395">FileAccessedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-395">FileAccessedExtended</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-396">这与“已访问文件”(FileAccessed) 活动有关。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-396">This is related to the "Accessed file" (FileAccessed) activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-397">如果一个用户长时间（至 3 小时）持续访问某一文件，则会记录下 FileAccessedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-397">A FileAccessedExtended event is logged when the same person continually accesses a file for an extended period (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-398">记录 FileAccessedExtended 事件是为了减少持续访问文件时所记录的 FileAccessed 事件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-398">The purpose of logging FileAccessedExtended events is to reduce the number of FileAccessed events that are logged when a file is continually accessed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-399">这有助于减小（实际上是）同一用户活动的多个 FileAccessed 记录的干扰，从而专注于初始（和更重要的）FileAccessed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-399">This helps reduce the noise of multiple FileAccessed records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) FileAccessed event.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-400">已更改合规性策略标签</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-400">Changed compliance policy label</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-401">ComplianceSettingChanged</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-401">ComplianceSettingChanged</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-402">保留标签已应用于文档或已从文档中删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-402">A retention label was applied to or removed from a document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-403">手动或自动将保留标签应用于消息时触发此事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-403">This event is triggered when a retention label is manually or automatically applied to a message.</span></span><br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-404">已将记录状态更改为“已锁定”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-404">Changed record status to locked</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-405">LockRecord</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-405">LockRecord</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-406">将文档分类为记录的保留标签的记录状态为“已锁定”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-406">The record status of a retention label that classifies a document as a record was locked.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-407">这意味着无法修改或删除文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-407">This means the document can't be modified or deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-408">仅至少分配有网站参与者权限的用户才能更改文档的记录状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-408">Only users assigned at least the contributor permission for a site can change the record status of a document.</span></span><br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-409">已将记录状态更改为“未锁定”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-409">Changed record status to unlocked</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-410">UnlockRecord</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-410">UnlockRecord</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-411">将文档分类为记录的保留标签的记录状态为“未锁定”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-411">The record status of a retention label that classifies a document as a record was unlocked.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-412">这意味着可以修改或删除文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-412">This means that the document can be modified or deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-413">仅至少分配有网站参与者权限的用户才能更改文档的记录状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-413">Only users assigned at least the contributor permission for a site can change the record status of a document.</span></span><br/><br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-414">已签入文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-414">Checked in file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-415">FileCheckedIn</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-415">FileCheckedIn\*</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-416">用户签入其从文档库中签出的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-416">User checks in a document that they checked out from a SharePoint or skydrive_pro document library.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-417">已签出文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-417">Checked out file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-418">FileCheckedOut</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-418">FileCheckedOut\*</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-419">用户签出位于文档库中的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-419">User checks out a document located in  a SharePoint or skydrive_pro document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-420">用户可以对与其共享的文档执行签出和更改操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-420">Users can check out and make changes to documents that have been shared with them.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-421">已复制文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-421">Copied file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-422">FileCopied</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-422">FileCopied</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-423">用户从网站复制文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-423">User copies a document  from a SharePoint or skydrive_pro site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-424">可以将复制的文件保存到网站上的另一个文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-424">The copied file can be saved to another folder on the site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-425">已删除文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-425">Deleted file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-426">FileDeleted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-426">FileDeleted</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-427">用户从网站删除文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-427">User deletes a document from a SharePoint or skydrive_pro site.</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-438">检测到文档敏感度不匹配</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-438">Detected document sensitivity mismatch</span></span> <br/>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-439">DocumentSensitivityMismatchDetected</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-439">DocumentSensitivityMismatchDetected</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-440">用户上传使用敏感度标签分类的文档，该标签的优先级高于将文档上传到的网站所应用的敏感度标签。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-440">User uploads a document classified with a sensitivity label that has a higher priority than the sensitivity label that's applied to the site the document is uploaded to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-441">如果应用于网站的敏感度标签优先级高于上传到网站的文档所应用的敏感度标签，则不会触发此事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-441">This event isn't triggered if the sensitivity label applied to a site has a higher priority than the sensitivity label applied to a document that's uploaded to the site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-442">有关敏感度标签优先级的详细信息，请参阅[敏感度标签概述](sensitivity-labels.md#label-priority-order-matters)中的“标签优先级”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-442">For more information about sensitivity label priority, see the "Label priority" section in [Overview of sensitivity labels](sensitivity-labels.md#label-priority-order-matters).</span></span><br/>|

That means any changes they made to the file when it was checked out are discarded, and not saved to the version of the document in the document library.</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-456">(无)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-456">(none)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-457">FileModifiedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-457">FileModifiedExtended</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-458">这与“已修改文件”(FileModified) 活动相关。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-458">This is related to the "Modified file" (FileModified) activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-459">如果一个用户长时间（至 3 小时）持续修改某一文件，则会记录下 FileModifiedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-459">A FileModifiedExtended event is logged when the same person continually modifies a file for an extended period (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-460">记录 FileModifiedExtended 事件是为了减少持续修改文件时所记录的 FileModified 事件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-460">The purpose of logging FileModifiedExtended events is to reduce the number of FileModified events that are logged when a file is continually modified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-461">这有助于减小（实际上是）同一用户活动的多个 FileModified 记录的干扰，从而专注于初始（和更重要的）FileModified 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-461">This helps reduce the noise of multiple FileModified records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) FileModified event.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-462">已移动文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-462">Moved a file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-463">FileMoved</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-463">FileMoved</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-464">用户将文档从网站上的当前位置移动到新位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-464">User moves a document  from its current location on a  SharePoint or skydrive_pro site to a new location..</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-469">已回收文件的次要版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-469">Recycled all minor versions of file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-470">FileVersionsAllMinorsRecycled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-470">FileVersionsAllMinorsRecycled</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-471">用户从文件版本历史记录中删除所有次要版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-471">User deletes all minor versions from the version history of a file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-472">已删除的版本移动到网站的回收站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-472">The deleted versions are moved to the site's recycle bin.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-473">已回收所有版本的文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-473">Recycled all versions of file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-474">FileVersionsAllRecycled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-474">FileVersionsAllRecycled</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-475">用户从文件版本历史记录中删除所有版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-475">User deletes all versions from the version history of a file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-476">已删除的版本移动到网站的回收站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-476">The deleted versions are moved to the site's recycle bin.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-477">已回收文件版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-477">Recycled version of file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-478">FileVersionRecycled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-478">FileVersionRecycled</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-479">用户从文件版本历史记录中删除某个版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-479">User deletes a version from the version history of a file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-480">已删除的版本移动到网站的回收站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-480">The deleted version is moved to the site's recycle bin.</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-490">已查看页面</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-490">Viewed page</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-491">PageViewed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-491">PageViewed</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-492">用户在网站上查看页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-492">User views a page on a SharePoint site or OneDrive for Business site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-493">这不包括使用 Web 浏览器查看位于文档库中的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-493">This doesn't include using a Web browser to view files located in a document library.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-494">(无)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-494">(none)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-495">PageViewedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-495">PageViewedExtended</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-496">这与“已查看页面”(PageViewed) 活动相关。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-496">This is related to the "Viewed page" (PageViewed) activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-497">如果一个用户长时间（至 3 小时）持续查看某一网页，则会记录下 PageViewedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-497">A PageViewedExtended event is logged when the same person continually views a web page for an extended period (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-498">记录 PageViewedExtended 事件是为了减少持续查看页面时所记录的 PageViewed 事件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-498">The purpose of logging PageViewedExtended events is to reduce the number of PageViewed events that are logged when a page is continually viewed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-499">这有助于减小（实际上是）同一用户活动的多个 PageViewed 记录的干扰，从而专注于初始（和更重要的）PageViewed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-499">This helps reduce the noise of multiple PageViewed records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) PageViewed event.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-500">按客户端查看信号</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-500">View signaled by client</span></span> <br/>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-501">ClientViewSignaled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-501">ClientViewSignaled</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-502">用户的客户端（例如网站或移动应用）已发出信号，表明用户已查看指示的页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-502">A user’s client (such as website or mobile app) has signaled that the indicated page has been viewed by the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-503">此活动通常在页面的 PagePrefetched 事件后记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-503">This activity is often logged following a PagePrefetched event for a page.</span></span> <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-504">**注意**：由于 ClientViewSignaled 事件由客户端而非服务器发出信号，因此服务器可能不会记录该事件，从而导致该事件可能未显示在审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-504">**NOTE**: Because ClientViewSignaled events are signaled by the client, rather than the server, it's possible the event may not be logged by the server and therefore may not appear in the audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-505">审核记录中的信息也可能不可信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-505">It's also possible that information in the audit record may not be trustworthy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-506">但是，由于用户身份由用于创建信号的令牌验证，因此相应审核记录中列出的用户身份是准确的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-506">However, because the user’s identity is validated by the token used to create the signal, the user’s identity listed in the corresponding audit record is accurate.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-507">(无)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-507">(none)</span></span> <br/>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-508">PagePrefetched</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-508">PagePrefetched</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-509">用户的客户端（例如网站或移动应用）已请求指示的页面，以帮助提高用户浏览时的性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-509">A user’s client (such as website or mobile app) has requested the indicated page to help improve performance if the user browses to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-510">记录此事件以指示页面内容已服务于用户的客户端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-510">This event is logged to indicate that the page content has been served to the user’s client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-511">此事件未明确指示用户导航到页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-511">This event isn't a definitive indication that the user navigated to the page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-512">当客户端（根据用户请求）呈现页面内容时，应生成 ClientViewSignaled 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-512">When the page content is rendered by the client (as per the user’s request) a ClientViewSignaled event should be generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-513">并非所有客户端都支持指示预提取，因此一些预提取的活动可能会被记录为 PageViewed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-513">Not all clients support indicating a pre-fetch, and therefore some pre-fetched activities might instead be logged as PageViewed events.</span></span><br/>|
||||
  
### <a name="folder-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-514">文件夹活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-514">Folder activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-515">下表介绍了 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的文件夹活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-515">The following table describes the folder activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span>
  
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-516">**友好名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-516">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-517">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-517">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-518">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-518">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-519">已复制文件夹</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-519">Copied folder</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-520">FolderCopied</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-520">FolderCopied</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-521">用户将文件夹从网站复制到 SharePoint 或 OneDrive for Business 的其他位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-521">User copies a folder from a SharePoint or OneDrive for Business site to another location in SharePoint or OneDrive for Business.</span></span>  <br/> |
