### <a name="sharing-and-access-request-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-620">共享和访问请求活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-620">Sharing and access request activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-621">下表介绍了 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的用户共享和访问请求活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-621">The following table describes the user sharing and access request activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-622">对于共享事件，“**结果**”下的“**详细信息**”列标识了与之共享项目的用户名或组名以及该用户或组是否为组织中的成员或来宾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-622">For sharing events, the **Detail** column under **Results** identifies the name of the user or group the item was shared with and whether that user or group is a member or guest in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-623">有关详细信息，请参阅[在 Office 365 审核日志中使用共享审核](use-sharing-auditing.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-623">For information about the SharePoint Sharing schema, see [Use sharing auditing in the Office 365 audit log](use-sharing-auditing.md).</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-624">根据用户对象的 UserType 属性，用户可以是*成员*或*来宾*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-624">Users can be either  *members*  or  *guests*  based on the UserType property of the user object.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-625">通常，成员为员工，来宾则为组织外部的合作者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-625">A member is usually an employee, and a guest is usually a collaborator outside of your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-626">用户接受共享邀请（而尚未成为你组织的一员）时，将在组织的目录中为其创建来宾帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-626">When a user accepts a sharing invitation (and isn't already part of your organization), a guest account is created for them in your organization's directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-627">来宾用户在你的目录中拥有帐户后，即可与其直接共享资源（无需邀请）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-627">Once the guest user has an account in your directory, resources may be shared directly with them (without requiring an invitation).</span></span> 
  
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-628">**友好名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-628">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-629">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-629">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-630">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-630">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-631">已向网站集添加权限级别</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-631">Added permission level to site collection</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-632">PermissionLevelAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-632">PermissionLevelAdded</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-633">已向网站集添加权限级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-633">A permission level was added to a site collection.</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="synchronization-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-720">同步活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-720">Synchronization activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-721">下表列出了 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的文件同步活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-721">The following table lists file synchronization activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span>
  
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-722">**友好名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-722">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-723">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-723">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-724">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-724">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-725">已允许计算机同步文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-725">Allowed computer to sync files</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-726">ManagedSyncClientAllowed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-726">ManagedSyncClientAllowed</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-727">用户成功建立与网站的同步关系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-727">User successfully establishes a sync relationship with a  SharePoint or skydrive_pro site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-728">同步关系之所以成功，是因为用户计算机是添加到域列表（称为*安全收件人列表*）的域成员，可以访问组织中的文档库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-728">The sync relationship is successful because the user's computer is a member of a domain that's been added to the list of domains (called the safe recipients list) that can access document libraries in your organization.</span></span>  <br/> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-729">有关此功能的详细信息，请参阅[使用 Windows PowerShell cmdlet 为安全收件人列表中的域启用 OneDrive 同步](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-729">For more information about this feature, see [Use Windows PowerShell cmdlets to enable OneDrive sync for domains that are on the safe recipients list](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-730">已阻止计算机同步文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-730">Blocked computer from syncing files</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-731">UnmanagedSyncClientBlocked</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-731">UnmanagedSyncClientBlocked</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-732">用户尝试从某计算机与网站建立同步关系，该计算机不是组织域的成员，或是尚未添加到可访问组织文档库的域列表（称为*安全收件人列表*）的域的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-732">User tries to establish a sync relationship with a SharePoint or OneDrive for Business site from a computer that isn't a member of your organization's domain or is a member of a domain that hasn't been added to the list of domains (called the safe recipients list) that can access document libraries in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-733">不允许同步关系，并阻止用户计算机在文档库上同步、下载或上传文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-733">The sync relationship is not allowed, and the user's computer is blocked from syncing, downloading, or uploading files on a document library.</span></span>  <br/> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-734">有关此功能的信息，请参阅[使用 Windows PowerShell cmdlet 为安全收件人列表中的域启用 OneDrive 同步](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-734">For information about this feature, see [Use Windows PowerShell cmdlets to enable OneDrive sync for domains that are on the safe recipients list](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-735">已将文件下载到计算机</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-735">Downloaded files to computer</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-736">FileSyncDownloadedFull</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-736">FileSyncDownloadedFull</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-737">用户建立同步关系，并首次成功将文件从文档库下载到计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-737">User establishes a sync relationship and successfully downloads files for the first time to their computer  from a SharePoint or skydrive_pro document library.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-738">已将文件更改下载到计算机</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-738">Downloaded file changes to computer</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-739">FileSyncDownloadedPartial</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-739">FileSyncDownloadedPartial</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-740">用户从文档库成功下载对文件所做的任何更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-740">User successfully downloads any changes to files from  SharePoint or skydrive_pro document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-741">此活动表明对文档库中的文件所做的任何更改均已被下载到用户计算机中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-741">This event indicates that any changes that were made to files in the document library were downloaded to the user's computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-742">仅下载了更改，因为用户以前下载过文档库（如**已将文件下载到计算机**活动所示）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-742">Only changes were downloaded because the document library was previously downloaded by the user (as indicated by the FileSyncDownloadedFull event).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-743">已将文件上传到文档库</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-743">Uploaded files to document library</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-744">FileSyncUploadedFull</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-744">FileSyncUploadedFull\*</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-745">用户建立同步关系，并首次成功将文件从计算机上传到文档库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-745">User establishes a sync relationship and successfully uploads  files for the first time from their computer to a SharePoint or skydrive_pro document library.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-746">已将文件更改上传到文档库</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-746">Uploaded file changes to document library</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-747">FileSyncUploadedPartial</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-747">FileSyncUploadedPartial\*</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-748">用户成功上传对文档库中的文件所做的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-748">User successfully uploads   changes to files  on a SharePoint or skydrive_pro document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-749">此事件表明对文档库文件的本地版本所做的任何更改都已成功上传到文档库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-749">This event indicates that any changes made to the local version of a file from a document library are successfully uploaded to the document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-750">仅已上传更改内容，因为用户以前上传过这些文件（如**已将文件上传到文档库**活动所示）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-750">Only changes are uploaded because those files were previously uploaded by the user (as indicated by the **Uploaded files to document library** activity).</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="site-permissions-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-751">网站权限活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-751">Site permissions activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-752">下表列出了与在 SharePoint 中分配权限以及使用组授予（和撤销）网站访问权限相关的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-752">The following table lists events related to assigning permissions in SharePoint and using groups to give (and revoke) access to sites.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-753">**友好名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-753">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-754">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-754">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-755">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-755">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-756">已添加网站集管理员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-756">Added site collection admin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-757">SiteCollectionAdminAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-757">SiteCollectionAdminAdded\*</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-758">网站集管理员或所有者为网站添加了作为网站集管理员的人员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-758">Site collection administrator or owner adds a person as a site collection administrator for a   SharePoint or skydrive_pro site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-759">网站集管理员具有网站集和所有子网站的完全控制权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-759">Site collection administrators have full control permissions for the site collection and all subsites.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-760">当管理员（通过在 SharePoint 管理中心编辑用户配置文件或[使用 Microsoft 365 管理中心](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data#part-1---get-access-to-the-former-employees-onedrive-for-business-documents)）向自己授予对用户 OneDrive 帐户的访问权限时，也将记录此活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-760">This activity is also logged when an admin gives themselves access to a user's OneDrive account (by editing the user profile in the SharePoint admin center or  [by using the Microsoft 365 admin center](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data#part-1---get-access-to-the-former-employees-onedrive-for-business-documents)).</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-761">已向 SharePoint 组添加用户或组</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-761">Added user or group to SharePoint group</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-762">AddedToGroup</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-762">AddedToGroup</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-763">用户向 SharePoint 组添加了成员或来宾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-763">User added a member or guest to a SharePoint group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-764">这可能是目的性操作，也可能是其他活动（例如共享事件）的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-764">This might have been an intentional action or the result of another activity, such as a sharing event.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-765">中断权限级别继承</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-765">Broke permission level inheritance</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-766">PermissionLevelsInheritanceBroken</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-766">PermissionLevelsInheritanceBroken</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-767">已更改项目，使其不再从父级继承权限级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-767">An item was changed so that it no longer inherits permission levels from its parent.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-768">中断共享继承</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-768">Broke sharing inheritance</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-769">SharingInheritanceBroken</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-769">SharingInheritanceBroken</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-770">已更改项目，使其不再从父级继承共享权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-770">An item was changed so that it no longer inherits sharing permissions from its parent.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-771">已创建组</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-771">Created group</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-772">GroupAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-772">GroupAdded\*</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-773">网站管理员或所有者为网站创建组，或执行将导致创建组的任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-773">Site administrator or owner  creates  a group  for a SharePoint or skydrive_pro site, or performs a task that results in a group being created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-774">例如，当用户首次创建共享文件的链接时，系统组会被添加到用户的 OneDrive for Business 网站中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-774">For example, the first time a user creates a link to share a file, a system group is added to the user's OneDrive for Business site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-775">此事件也可以是用户使用编辑权限创建共享文件链接的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-775">This event can also be a result of a user creating a link with edit permissions to a shared file.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-776">已删除组</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-776">Deleted group objects.</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-777">GroupRemoved</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-777">GroupRemoved\*</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-778">用户从网站删除组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-778">User deletes  a group from a SharePoint or skydrive_pro site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-779">已修改访问请求设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-779">Modified access request setting</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-780">WebRequestAccessModified</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-780">WebRequestAccessModified</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-781">已修改网站上的访问请求设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-781">The access request settings were modified on a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-782">已修改“成员可共享”设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-782">Modified 'Members Can Share' setting</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-783">WebMembersCanShareModified</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-783">WebMembersCanShareModified</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-784">已修改网站上的“**成员可共享**”设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-784">The **Members Can Share** setting was modified on a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-785">已修改网站集的权限级别</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-785">Modified permission level on site collection</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-786">PermissionLevelModified</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-786">PermissionLevelModified</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-787">已更改网站集的权限级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-787">A permission level was changed on a site collection.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-788">已修改网站权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-788">Modified site permissions</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-789">SitePermissionsModified</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-789">SitePermissionsModified</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-790">网站管理员或所有者（或系统帐户）更改分配给网站上的组的权限级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-790">Site administrator or owner  (or system account) changes the permission level that are assigned to a group on a  SharePoint or skydrive_pro site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-791">如果从组中删除所有权限，也将记录此活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-791">This event is also logged if all permissions are removed from a group.</span></span>  <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-792">**注意**：SharePoint Online 中已弃用此操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-792">**NOTE**: This operation has been deprecated in SharePoint Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-793">若要查找相关事件，可搜索其他权限相关的活动，例如**已添加网站集管理员**、**已向 SharePoint 组添加用户或组**、**已允许用户创建组**、**已创建组**和**已删除组**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-793">To find related events, you can search for other permission-related activities such as **Added site collection admin**, **Added user or group to SharePoint group**, **Allowed user to create groups**, **Created group**, and **Deleted group.**</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-794">已删除网站集的权限级别</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-794">Removed permission level from site collection</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-795">PermissionLevelRemoved</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-795">PermissionLevelRemoved</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-796">已删除网站集的权限级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-796">A permission level was removed from a site collection.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-797">已删除网站集管理员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-797">Removed site collection admin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-798">SiteCollectionAdminRemoved</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-798">SiteCollectionAdminRemoved</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-799">网站集管理员或所有者为网站删除了作为网站集管理员的人员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-799">Site collection administrator or owner adds a person as a site collection administrator for a   SharePoint or skydrive_pro site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-800">当管理员（通过在 SharePoint 管理中心编辑用户配置文件）从用户 OneDrive 帐户的网站集管理员列表中删除自己时，也会记录此活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-800">This activity is also logged when an admin removes themselves from the list of site collection administrators for a user's OneDrive account (by editing the user profile in the SharePoint admin center).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="3863b-801">若要在审核日志搜索结果中返回此活动，必须搜索所有活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-801">To return this activity in the audit log search results, you have to search for all activities.</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-802">已从 SharePoint 组中删除用户或组</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-802">Removed user or group from SharePoint group</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-803">RemovedFromGroup</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-803">RemovedFromGroup</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-804">用户已从 SharePoint 组中删除成员或来宾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-804">User removed a member or guest from a SharePoint group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-805">这可能是一项目的性操作，也可能是其他活动（例如取消共享事件）的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-805">This might have been an intentional action or the result of another activity, such as an unsharing event.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-806">已请求网站管理员权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-806">Requested site admin permissions</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-807">SiteAdminChangeRequest</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-807">SiteAdminChangeRequest\*</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-808">用户请求将自己添加为网站集的网站集管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-808">User requests to be added as a site collection administrator for a SharePoint site collection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-809">网站集管理员具有网站集和所有子网站的完全控制权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-809">Site collection administrators have full control permissions for the site collection and all subsites.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-810">已还原共享继承</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-810">Restored sharing inheritance</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-811">SharingInheritanceReset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-811">SharingInheritanceReset</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-812">已进行更改，使项目能够从父级继承共享权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-812">A change was made so that an item inherits sharing permissions from its parent.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-813">已更新组</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-813">Updated group</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-814">GroupUpdated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-814">GroupUpdated\*</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-815">网站管理员或所有者为网站更改组设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-815">Site administrator or owner  changes the settings of a  group  for a SharePoint or skydrive_pro site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-816">这可能包括更改组名、可以查看或编辑组成员身份的人员，以及成员身份请求的处理方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-816">This can include changing the group's name, who can view or edit the group membership, and how membership requests are handled.</span></span>  <br/> |
||||

  
### <a name="site-administration-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-817">网站管理活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-817">Site administration activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-818">下表列出了 SharePoint Online 中的网站管理任务所产生的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-818">The following table lists the   events that result from site administration tasks in SharePoint and skydrive_pro.</span></span>
  
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-819">**友好名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-819">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-820">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-820">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-821">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-821">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-822">已添加允许的数据位置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-822">Added allowed data location</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-823">AllowedDataLocationAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-823">AllowedDataLocationAdded</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-824">SharePoint 或全局管理员在多地理环境中添加了允许的数据位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-824">A SharePoint or global administrator added an allowed data location in a multi-geo environment.</span></span> <br/>|
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-825">已添加豁免用户代理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-825">Added exempt user agent</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-826">ExemptUserAgentSet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-826">ExemptUserAgentSet\*</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-827">SharePoint 或全局管理员向 SharePoint 管理中心的豁免用户代理列表添加了用户代理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-827">Global administrator adds a user agent to the list of exempt user agents in the SharePoint admin center.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-828">已添加地理位置管理员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-828">Added geo location admin</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-829">GeoAdminAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-829">GeoAdminAdded</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-830">SharePoint 或全局管理员已将用户添加为地理位置管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-830">A SharePoint or global administrator added a user as a geo admin of a location.</span></span> <br/>|

|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-834">已取消网站地域移动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-834">Cancelled site geo move</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-835">SiteGeoMoveCancelled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-835">SiteGeoMoveCancelled</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-836">SharePoint 或全局管理员成功取消 SharePoint 或 OneDrive 网站地域移动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-836">A SharePoint or global administrator successfully cancels a SharePoint or OneDrive site geo move.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-837">多地理位置功能可让一个 Office 365 组织跨越多个 Office 365 数据中心地理位置（称之为地理位置）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-837">The Multi-Geo capability lets an Office_365 organization span  multiple Office_365 datacenter geographies, which are called geos.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-838">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Office 365 中 OneDrive 和 SharePoint Online 的多地理位置功能](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=860840)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-838">For more information about Multi-Geo Capabilities in OneDrive and SharePoint Online in Office 365, click [here](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=860840).</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-850">已更改豁免用户代理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-850">Changed exempt user agents</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-851">CustomizeExemptUsers</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-851">CustomizeExemptUsers\*</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-852">SharePoint 或全局管理员自定义 SharePoint 管理中心的豁免用户代理列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-852">Global administrator customized the list of exempt user agents in SharePoint admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-853">你可以指定免于接收要索引的整个网页的用户代理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-853">You can specify which user agents to exempt from receiving an entire web page to index.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-854">这意味着，当指定为豁免的用户代理遇到 InfoPath 表单时，表单将作为 XML 文件而不是整个网页返回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-854">This means when a user agent you've specified as exempt encounters an InfoPath form, the form will be returned as an XML file instead of an entire Web page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-855">这可以加速对 InfoPath 表单编制索引。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-855">This makes indexing InfoPath forms faster.</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="exchange-mailbox-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-936">Exchange 邮箱活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-936">Exchange mailbox activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-937">下表列出了可以由邮箱审核日志记录的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-937">The following table lists the actions performed by non-owners that can be logged by mailbox audit logging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-938">在 Office 365 审核日志中自动将由邮箱所有者、委派用户或管理员执行的邮箱活动记录长达 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-938">Mailbox activities performed by the mailbox owner, a delegated user, or an administrator are automatically logged in the Office 365 audit log for up to 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-939">管理员可以为组织中的所有用户关闭邮箱审核日志记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-939">It's possible for an admin to turn off mailbox audit logging for all users in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-940">在这种情况下, ，不会记录任何用户的邮箱操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-940">In this case, no mailbox actions for any user are logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-941">有关详细信息，请参阅[管理邮箱审核](enable-mailbox-auditing.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-941">For more information, see [Manage on-premises mailbox moves in Exchange 2016](enable-mailbox-auditing.md).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="3863b-942">你还可以使用 Exchange Online PowerShell 中的 [Search-MailboxAuditLog](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/policy-and-compliance-audit/search-mailboxauditlog) cmdlet 来搜索邮箱活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-942">You can also search for mailbox activities by using the [Search-MailboxAuditLog](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/policy-and-compliance-audit/search-mailboxauditlog) cmdlet in Exchange Online PowerShell.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-995">已删除代理邮箱权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-995">Removed delegate mailbox permissions</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-996">Remove-MailboxPermission</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-996">Remove-MailboxPermission</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-997">管理员已从用户邮箱删除分配给代理的 FullAccess 权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-997">An administrator removed the FullAccess permission (that was assigned to a delegate) from a person's mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-998">删除 FullAccess 权限后，代理无法打开他人邮箱，也无法访问该邮箱中的任何内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-998">After the FullAccess permission is removed, the delegate can't open the other person's mailbox or access any content in it.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-999">已从文件夹中删除权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-999">Removed permissions from folder</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1000">RemoveFolderPermissions</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1000">RemoveFolderPermissions</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1001">已删除文件夹权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1001">A folder permission was removed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1002">文件夹权限用于控制组织中的哪些用户可以访问邮箱中的文件夹以及位于这些文件夹中的邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1002">Folder permissions control which users in your organization can access folders in a mailbox and the messages located in those folders.</span></span><br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1003">已使用“发送方式”权限发送邮件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1003">A message is sent using Send As permissions.</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1004">SendAs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1004">SendAs</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1005">已使用“发送方式”权限发送邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1005">A message was sent using SendAs permission.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1006">这表示另一个用户发送了邮件，而该邮件就好像来自于邮箱所有者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1006">This means another user sent the message as though it came from the mailbox owner.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1007">已使用“代表发送”权限发送邮件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1007">Sent message using Send On Behalf permissions</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1008">SendOnBehalf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1008">SendOnBehalf</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1009">已使用“代表发送”权限发送邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1009">A message was sent using SendOnBehalf permission.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1010">这表示另一个用户代表邮箱所有者发送了邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1010">This means another user sent the message on behalf of the mailbox owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1011">邮件将向收件人说明发送此邮件时使用的身份及实际发送者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1011">The message will indicate to the recipient who the message was sent on behalf of and who actually sent the message.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1012">已从 Outlook 客户端更新收件箱规则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1012">Updated inbox rules from Outlook client</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1013">UpdateInboxRules</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1013">UpdateInboxRules operation</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1014">有权访问邮箱的邮箱所有者或其他用户在 Outlook 客户端中修改了收件箱规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1014">A mailbox owner or other user with access to the mailbox modified an inbox rule in the Outlook client.</span></span><br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1015">已更新邮件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1015">Updated message</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1016">更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1016">Update</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1017">已更改邮件或其属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1017">A message or its properties was changed.</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="sway-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1021">Sway 活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1021">Sway activities</span></span>

### <a name="ediscovery-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1215">电子数据展示活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1215">eDiscovery activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1216">在安全与合规中心中执行或通过运行相应 PowerShell cmdlet 执行的内容搜索和电子数据展示相关活动将记录在审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1216">Content Search and eDiscovery-related activities that are performed in the security and compliance center or by running the corresponding PowerShell cmdlets are logged in the audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1217">这包括下列活动：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1217">This includes the following:</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1218">创建和管理电子数据展示事例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1218">Creating and managing eDiscovery cases</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1219">创建、启动和编辑“内容搜索”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1219">Creating, starting, and editing Content Searches</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1220">执行“内容搜索”操作，如预览、导出和删除搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1220">Performing Content Search actions, such as previewing, exporting, and deleting search results</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1221">为“内容搜索”配置权限筛选</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1221">Configure permissions filtering for Content Search</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1222">管理电子数据展示管理员角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1222">Managing the eDiscovery Administrator role</span></span>
    
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1223">有关记录的电子数据展示活动的列表和详细说明，请参阅[搜索 Office 365 审核日志中的电子数据展示活动](search-for-ediscovery-activities-in-the-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1223">For a list and detailed description of the eDiscovery activities that are logged, see [Search for eDiscovery activities in the Office 365 audit log](search-for-ediscovery-activities-in-the-audit-log.md).</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1224">“**活动**”下拉列表中“**电子数据展示活动**”下列出的活动结果需要最多 30 分钟即可显示在搜索结果中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1224">It takes up to 30 minutes for events that result from the activities listed under **eDiscovery activities** in the **Activities** drop-down list to be displayed in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1225">相反，电子数据展示 cmdlet 活动的相应事件需要长达 24 小时才可显示在搜索结果中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1225">Conversely, it takes up to 24 hours for the corresponding events from eDiscovery cmdlet activities to appear in the search results.</span></span> 
  
### <a name="advanced-ediscovery-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1226">高级电子数据展示活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1226">Advanced eDiscovery activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1227">下表列出了 IT 和法律专业人员在 Microsoft 365 高级电子数据展示中执行任务所产生的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1227">The following table lists activities that result from IT and legal professionals performing tasks in Advanced eDiscovery in Microsoft 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1228">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Microsoft 365 中的高级电子数据展示解决方案概述](compliance20/overview-ediscovery-20.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1228">For more information, see [Overview of the Advanced eDiscovery solution in Microsoft 365](compliance20/overview-ediscovery-20.md).</span></span>

### <a name="power-bi-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1306">Power BI 活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1306">Power BI activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1307">可以在审核日志中搜索 Power BI 内的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1307">You can search the audit log for activities in Power BI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1308">有关 Power BI 活动的信息，请参阅[在组织内部使用审核](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-auditing#activities-audited-by-power-bi)中的“Power BI 审核的活动”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1308">For information about Power BI activities, see the "Activities audited by Power BI" section in [Using auditing within your organization](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-auditing#activities-audited-by-power-bi).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1309">默认情况下，Power BI 的审核日志记录未启用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1309">Audit logging for Power BI isn't enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1310">若要在 Office 365 审核日志中搜索 Power BI 活动，必须在 Power BI 管理门户中启用审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1310">To search for Power BI activities in the Office 365 audit log, you have to enable auditing in the Power BI admin portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1311">有关说明，请参阅 [Power BI 管理门户](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs)中的“审核日志”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1311">For instructions, see the "Audit logs" section in [Power BI admin portal](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs).</span></span>

Skype 会议屏幕共享 **”）。<br/><br/>- 允许或禁止将动画图像（称为 Giphys）添加到 Teams 对话（“动画图像**”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1390">- Enables or disables video calling in Teams meetings (Video for Skype meetings **).  <br/><br/>- Enables or disables screen sharing in Microsoft Teams meetups for the organization (** Screen sharing for Skype meetings **).  <br/><br/>- Enables or disables that ability to add animated images (called Giphys) to Teams conversations (Animated images**).</span></span>  <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1391">- 更改组织的内容评级设置（“**内容评级**”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1391">- Changes the content rating setting for the organization (**Content rating**).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1392">内容评级限制了可在对话中显示的动画图像的类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1392">The content rating restricts the type of animated image that can be displayed in conversations.</span></span>  <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1393">- 允许或禁止团队成员将来自 Internet 的可自定义图像（称为自定义 Meme）添加到团队对话（“来自 Internet 的可自定义图像 **”）。<br/><br/>- 允许或禁止团队成员将可编辑图像（称为贴纸）添加到团队对话（“** 可编辑图像 **”）。<br/><br/>- 允许或禁止团队成员在 Microsoft Teams 聊天和频道中使用机器人（“组织范围内的机器人**”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1393">-   Enables or disables the ability for team members to add customizable images (called custom memes) from the Internet to team conversations (Customizable images from the Internet **).  <br/><br/>- Enables or disables the ability for team members to add editable images (called stickers) to team conversations (** Editable images **).<br/><br/>- Enables or disables that ability for team members to use bots in Microsoft Teams chats and channels (Org-wide bots**).</span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1394">- 为 Microsoft Teams 启用特定的机器人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1394">- Enables specific bots for Microsoft Teams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1395">这不包括 T-Bot，即组织启用机器人时可用的 Teams 帮助机器人（“**单个机器人**”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1395">This doesn't include the T-Bot, which is Teams help bot that's available when bots are enabled for the organization (**Individual bots**).</span></span>  <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1396">- 允许或禁止团队成员添加扩展或选项卡（“**扩展或选项卡**”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1396">- Enables or disables the ability for team members to add extensions or tabs (**Extensions or tabs**).</span></span>  <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1397">- 启用或禁用 Microsoft Teams 专有自动程序旁加载（“**自动程序旁加载**”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1397">- Enables or disables the side-loading of proprietary Bots for Microsoft Teams (**Side loading of Bots**).</span></span>  <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1398">- 允许或禁止用户向 Microsoft Teams 频道发送电子邮件（“**频道电子邮件**”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1398">- Enables or disables the ability for users to send email messages to a Microsoft Teams channel (**Channel email**).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1399">已更改团队成员的角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1399">Changed role of members in team</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1400">MemberRoleChanged</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1400">MemberRoleChanged</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1401">团队所有者更改团队中成员的角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1401">A team owner changes the role of members in a team.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1402">以下值表示分配给用户的角色类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1402">The following values indicate the Role type assigned to the user.</span></span>  <br/><br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1403">**1** - 表示“所有者”角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1403">**1** - Indicates the Owner role.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1404">**2** - 表示“成员”角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1404">**2** -   Indicates the Member role.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1405">**3** - 表示“来宾”角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1405">**3** - Indicates the Guest role.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1406">成员属性还包括组织的名称和成员的电子邮件地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1406">The Members property also includes the name of your organization, and the member's email address.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1407">已更改的团队设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1407">Changed team setting</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1408">TeamSettingChanged</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1408">TeamSettingChanged</span></span>  <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1409">团队所有者执行以下活动时将记录 TeamSettingChanged 操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1409">The TeamSettingChanged operation is logged when the following activities are performed by a team owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1410">对于每个活动，审核日志搜索结果中的“**项目**”列将显示已更改设置的说明（显示在下方括号中）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1410">For each of these activities, a description of the setting that was changed (shown in parentheses below) is displayed in the **Item** column in the audit log search results.</span></span>  <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1411">- 更改团队的访问权限类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1411">- Changes the access type for a team.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1412">可将团队设置为“专用​​”或“公用”（“**团队访问权限类型**”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1412">Teams can be set as Private or Public (**Team access type**).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1413">当团队为专用（默认设置）时，用户只能通过邀请访问该团队。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1413">When a team is private (the default setting), users can access the team only by invitation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1414">当团队为公用时，任何人都可以发现它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1414">When a team is public, it's discoverable by anyone.</span></span>  <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1415">- 更改团队的信息分类（“**团队分类**”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1415">- Changes the information classification of a team (**Team classification**).</span></span>  <br/>  <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1416">例如，可将团队数据分类为高业务影响、中等业务影响或低业务影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1416">For example, team data can be classified as high business impact, medium business impact, or low business impact.</span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1417">- 更改团队的名称（“**团队名称**”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1417">- Changes the name of a team (**Team name**).</span></span>  <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1418">- 更改团队说明（“团队说明”\*\*）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1418">- Changes the team description (Team description\*\*).</span></span> <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1419">- 更改任何团队设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1419">- Changes made to any of the team settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1420">团队所有者可通过右键单击某个团队，单击“**管理团队**”，然后单击“**设置**”选项卡在 Teams 客户端中访问这些设置。对于这些活动，审核日志搜索结果中的“**项目**”列将显示已更改设置的名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1420">A team owner can access these settings in a Teams client by right-clicking a team, clicking **Manage team**, and then clicking the **Settings** tab. ### <a name="yammer-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1451">Yammer 活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1451">Yammer activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1452">下表列出了 Yammer 中记录在 Office 365 审核日志中的用户和管理员活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1452">The following table lists the user and admin activities in Yammer that are logged in the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1453">若要从 Office 365 审核日志返回到与 Yammer 相关的活动，必须选择“**活动**”列表中的“**显示所有活动的结果**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1453">To return Yammer-related activities from the Office 365 audit log, you have to select **Show results for all activities** in the **Activities** list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1454">使用日期范围框和“**用户**”列表，缩小搜索结果的范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1454">Use the date range   boxes and the **Display results for these users**   drop down list to narrow the search results for audit  log entries for a specific mailbox.</span></span> 
  
|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1455">**友好名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1455">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1456">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1456">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1457">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1457">**Description**</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1462">已更改网络配置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1462">Changed network configuration</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1463">NetworkConfigurationUpdated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1463">NetworkConfigurationUpdated</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1464">网络管理员或验证管理员更改了 Yammer 网络的配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1464">Network or verified admin changes the Yammer network's configuration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1465">其中包括设置了导出数据和启用聊天室的时间间隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1465">This includes setting the interval for exporting data and enabling chat.</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1469">已更改私密内容模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1469">Changed private content mode</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1470">SupervisorAdminToggled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1470">SupervisorAdminToggled</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1471">验证管理员启用或禁用了“*私密内容模式*”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1471">Verified admin turns  *Private Content Mode*  on or off.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1472">此模式使管理员能够在专用组中查看公告并可在个人用户（或用户组）之间查看私人消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1472">This mode lets an admin view the posts in private groups and view private messages between individual users (or groups of users).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1473">只有验证管理员可执行此操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1473">Only verified admins only can perform this operation.</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="microsoft-flow-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1516">Microsoft Flow 活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1516">Microsoft Flow activities</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-powerapps"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1520">Microsoft PowerApps</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1520">Microsoft PowerApps</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-stream-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1525">Microsoft Stream 活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1525">Microsoft Stream activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1526">可以在审核日志中搜索 Microsoft Stream 内的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1526">You can search the audit log for activities in Microsoft Stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1527">这些活动包括用户执行的视频活动、组频道活动和管理员活动，例如管理用户、管理组织设置和导出报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1527">These activities include video activities performed by users, group channel activities, and admin activities such as managing users, managing organization settings, and exporting reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1528">有关这些活动的说明，请参阅 [Microsoft Stream 中的审核日志](https://docs.microsoft.com/stream/audit-logs)的“Microsoft Stream 中记录的活动”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1528">For a description of these activities, see the "Activities logged in Microsoft Stream" section in [Audit Logs in Microsoft Stream](https://docs.microsoft.com/stream/audit-logs).</span></span>

### <a name="exchange-admin-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1529">Exchange 管理员审核日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1529">Events from the Exchange admin audit log.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1530">管理员（或已分配到管理权限的用户）在 Exchange Online 组织中做出更改时，Exchange 管理员审核日志记录（Office 365 中默认启用此功能）将在 Office 365 审核日志中记录事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1530">Exchange administrator audit logging (which is enabled by default in Office 365) logs an event in the Office 365 audit log when an administrator (or a user who has been assigned administrative permissions) makes a change in your Exchange Online organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1531">通过使用 Exchange 管理中心所做的更改或通过运行 Exchange Online PowerShell 中的某个 cmdlet 所做的更改会记录在 Exchange 管理员审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1531">Changes made by using the Exchange admin center or by running a cmdlet in WindowsPowerShell are logged in the Exchange admin audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1532">以动词 **Get-**、**Search-** 或 **Test-** 开头的 Cmdlet 未记录在 Office 365 审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1532">Cmdlets that begin with the verbs **Get-**, **Search-**, or **Test-** are not logged in the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1533">有关 Exchange 中管理员审核日志记录的更多详细信息，请参阅[管理员审核日志记录](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=619225)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1533">For more detailed information about admin audit logging in Exchange, see  Administrator audit logging http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=619225 .</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1534">某些 Exchange Online cmdlet 未记录在 Exchange 管理员审核日志中（或 Office 365 审核日志中）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1534">Some Exchange Online cmdlets that aren't logged in the Exchange admin audit log (or in the Office 365 audit log).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1535">其中许多 cmdlet 都与维护 Exchange Online 服务有关，并由 Microsoft 数据中心人员或服务帐户运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1535">Many of these cmdlets are related to maintaining the Exchange Online service and are run by Microsoft datacenter personnel or service accounts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1536">未记录这些 cmdlet，因为它们会导致大量“嘈杂”的审核事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1536">These cmdlets aren't logged because they would result in a large number of "noisy" auditing events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1537">如果存在未经审核的 Exchange Online cmdlet，请向 [Office 365 安全与合规用户之声论坛](https://office365.uservoice.com/forums/289138-office-365-security-compliance)提交建议，并请求进行审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1537">If there's an Exchange Online cmdlet that isn't being audited, please submit a suggestion to the [Office 365 Security & Compliance User Voice forum](https://office365.uservoice.com/forums/289138-office-365-security-compliance) and request that it is enabled for auditing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1538">你还可以向 Microsoft 支持部门提交设计更改请求 (DCR)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1538">You can also submit a design change request (DCR) to Microsoft Support.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1539">以下是在搜索 Office 365 审核日志时搜索 Exchange 管理员活动的一些提示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1539">Here are some tips for searching for Exchange admin activities when searching the Office 365 audit log:</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1540">若要返回 Exchange 管理员审核日志中的条目，必须选择“**活动**”列表中的“**显示所有活动的结果**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1540">To return entries from the Exchange admin audit log, you have to select All activities in the user activity list in the O365_W14_2nd activity report.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1541">使用日期范围框和“**用户**”列表缩小由特定 Exchange 管理员在特定日期范围内运行的 cmdlet 的搜索结果范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1541">Use the date range   boxes and the Display results for these users   drop down list to narrow the search results for audit log entries for cmdlets run by a specific Exchange  administrator.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1542">若要显示 Exchange 管理员审核日志中的事件，请筛选搜索结果并在“**活动**”筛选器框中键入 **-**（破折号）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1542">To display events from the Exchange admin audit log, filter the search results and type a **-** (dash) in the **Activity** filter box.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1543">这将在 Exchange 管理员事件的“**活动**”列中显示 cmdlet 名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1543">This displays cmdlet names, which are displayed in the **Activity** column for Exchange admin events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1544">然后你便可按字母顺序对 cmdlet 名称进行排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1544">Then you can sort the cmdlet names in alphabetical order.</span></span> 
    
    ![在“活动”框中键入一个破折号以筛选 Exchange 管理事件](media/7628e7aa-6263-474a-a28b-2dcf5694bb27.png)
  
- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1546">若要获取有关已运行的 cmdlet、已使用的参数和参数值以及受影响对象的信息，可以导出搜索结果并选择“**下载所有结果**”选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1546">To get information about what cmdlet was run, which parameters and parameter values were used, and what objects were affected, you can export the search results by selecting the **Download all results** option.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1547">有关详细信息，请参阅[导出、配置和查看审核日志记录](export-view-audit-log-records.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1547">For more information, see [Export, configure, and view audit log records](export-view-audit-log-records.md).</span></span> 

- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1548">你还可以使用 Exchange Online PowerShell 中的 `Search-UnifiedAuditLog -RecordType ExchangeAdmin` 命令仅从 Exchange 管理员审核日志中返回审核记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1548">You can also use the `Search-UnifiedAuditLog -RecordType ExchangeAdmin` command in Exchange Online PowerShell to return only audit records from the Exchange admin audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1549">运行 Exchange cmdlet 后，可能需要长达 30 分钟的时间在搜索结果中返回相应的审核日志条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1549">It may take up to 30 minutes after a Exchange cmdlet is run for the corresponding audit log entry to be returned in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1550">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Search-UnifiedAuditLog](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/policy-and-compliance-audit/search-unifiedauditlog)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1550">For more information, see:[](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/policy-and-compliance-audit/search-unifiedauditlog)</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1551">有关将 **Search-UnifiedAuditLog** cmdlet 所返回的搜索结果导出到 CSV 文件的信息，请参阅[导出、配置和查看审核日志记录](export-view-audit-log-records.md#tips-for-exporting-and-viewing-the-audit-log)中的“有关导出和查看审核日志的提示”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1551">For information about exporting the search results returned by the **Search-UnifiedAuditLog** cmdlet to a CSV file, see the "Tips for exporting and viewing the audit log" section in [Export, configure, and view audit log records](export-view-audit-log-records.md#tips-for-exporting-and-viewing-the-audit-log).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1552">你还可以使用 Exchange 管理中心或在 Exchange Online PowerShell 中运行 **Search-AdminAuditLog** 来查看 Exchange 管理员审核日志中的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1552">You can also view events in the Exchange admin audit log by using the Exchange admin center or running the **Search-AdminAuditLog** in Exchange Online PowerShell.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1553">这是一种具体搜索由 Exchange Online 管理员执行的活动的好方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1553">This is a good way to specifically search for activity performed by Exchange Online administrators.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1554">有关说明，请参阅以下内容：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1554">For instructions, see:</span></span>
   
   - [<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1555">查看管理员审核日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1555">View the administrator audit log</span></span>](https://technet.microsoft.com/library/dn342832%28v=exchg.150%29.aspx) 
   
   -  [<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1556">Search-AdminAuditLog</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1556">Search-AdminAuditLog</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/policy-and-compliance-audit/search-adminauditlog)
   
   <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1557">请记住，Exchange 管理员审核日志和 Office 365 审核日志中记录了相同的 Exchange 管理员活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1557">Keep in mind that the same Exchange admin activities are logged in both the Exchange admin audit log and and Office 365 audit log.</span></span>
  
## <a name="frequently-asked-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="3863b-1558">常见问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1558">Frequently asked questions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1559">**从哪里可以了解 Office 365 中的审核服务提供的功能？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1559">**Where can I find about the features offered by the auditing service in Office 365?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1560">有关 Office 365 中提供的审核和报告功能的详细信息，请参阅 [Office 365 中的审核和报告](office-365-auditing-and-reporting-overview.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1560">For more information about the auditing and reporting features available in Office 365, see [Auditing and Reporting in Office 365](office-365-auditing-and-reporting-overview.md).</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1561">**目前审核的各种 Office 365 服务有哪些？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1561">**What are different Office 365 services that are currently audited?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1562">已审核最常用的 Office 365 服务，例如 Exchange Online、SharePoint Online、OneDrive for Business、Azure Active Directory、Microsoft Teams、Dynamics 365、高级威胁防护和 Power BI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1562">The most used Office 365 services like Exchange Online, SharePoint Online, OneDrive for Business, Azure Active Directory, Microsoft Teams, Dynamics 365, Advanced Threat Protection, and Power BI are audited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1563">有关已审核的服务列表，请参阅[本文开头部分](search-the-audit-log-in-security-and-compliance.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1563">See the [beginning of this article](search-the-audit-log-in-security-and-compliance.md) for a list of services that are audited.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1564">**哪些活动由 Office 365 中的审核服务进行审核？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1564">**What activities are audited by auditing service in Office 365?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1565">有关在 Office 365 中审核的活动列表和说明，请参阅本文[已审核的活动](#audited-activities)部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1565">See the [Audited activities](#audited-activities) section in this article for a list and description of the activities that are audited in Office 365.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1566">**审核记录在事件发生后的多长时间内可用？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1566">**How long does it take for an auditing record to be available after an event has occurred?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1567">发生事件后，大部分审核数据在 30 分钟内可用，但最长可能需要 24 小时才能在搜索结果中显示相应的审核日志条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1567">Most auditing data is available within 30 minutes but it may take up to 24 hours after an event occurs for the corresponding audit log entry to be displayed in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1568">请参阅本文[开始之前](#before-you-begin)部分中的表格，其中显示了各种 Office 365 服务提供事件审核记录所需的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1568">See the table in the [Before you begin](#before-you-begin) section of this article that shows the time it takes for events in the different Office 365 services to be available.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1569">**审核记录将保留多长时间？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1569">**How long are the audit records retained for?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1570">如前文所述，审核记录的保留期取决于组织的 Office 365 订阅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1570">As previously explained, the retention period for audit records depends on your organization's Office 365 subscription.</span></span>  

- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1571">**Office 365 E3：** 审核记录可保留 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1571">**Office 365 E3:** Audit records are retained for 90 days.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1572">**Office 365 E5：** 审核记录也可保留 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1572">**Office 365 E5:** Audit records are also retained for 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1573">对于 E5 用户以及具有 E3 许可证和 Office 365 高级合规版附加许可证的用户，最终可将审核记录保留一年。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1573">Retaining audit records for one year may eventually be available for E5 users and users with an E3 license and an Office 365 Advanced Compliance add-on license.</span></span>

     > [!NOTE]
     > <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1574">如上文所述，对于 E5 组织（或具有高级合规版附加许可证的 E3 组织），针对审核记录的一年保留期的个人预览版计划已对新注册关闭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1574">As previously explained, the private preview program for the one-year retention period for audit records for E5 organizations (or E3 organizations that have Advanced Compliance add-on licenses) is closed to new enrollment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1575">当公共预览版提供一年保留期或正式发布时，本文将更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1575">This article will be updated when the one-year retention period is available in public preview or released for general availability.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1576">另请注意，审核记录的保留期限基于每位用户许可。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1576">Also note that the duration of the retention period for audit records is based on per-user licensing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1577">例如，如果为组织内的用户分配了 Office 365 E3 或 E5 许可证，则该用户执行的活动的审核记录将保留 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1577">For example, if a user in your organization is assigned an Office 365 E3 or E5 license, then the audit records for activities performed by that user are retained for 90 days.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1578">**我是否可以通过编程方式访问审核数据？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1578">**Can I access the auditing data programmatically?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1579">是。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1579">Yes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1580">Office 365 管理活动 API 用于以编程方式获取审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1580">The Office 365 Management Activity API is used to fetch the audit logs programmatically.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1581">若要开始使用，请参阅 [Office 365 管理 API 入门](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/get-started-with-office-365-management-apis)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1581">To get started with the Office 365 Management Activity API, see [Get started with Office 365 Management APIs](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/get-started-with-office-365-management-apis).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1582">**除了使用安全与合规中心或 Office 365 管理活动 API 之外，是否还有其他方法可以获取审核日志？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1582">**Are there other ways to get auditing logs other than using the security and compliance center or the Office 365 Management Activity API?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1583">否。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1583">No.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1584">以下是从 Office 365 审核服务获取数据的两种方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1584">These are the only two ways to get data from the Office 365 auditing service.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1585">**是否需要在每个要捕获审核日志的服务中单独启用审核？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1585">**Do I need to individually enable auditing in each service that I want to capture audit logs for?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1586">在大多数 Office 365 服务中，在首次为 Office 365 组织启用审核后将默认启用审核功能（如本文[开始之前](#before-you-begin)部分所述）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1586">In most Office 365 services, auditing is enabled by default after you initially turn on auditing for your Office 365 organization (as described in the [Before you begin](#before-you-begin) section in this article).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1587">**Office 365 审核服务是否支持记录的重复数据删除？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1587">**Does the Office 365 auditing service support de-duplication of records?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1588">否。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1588">No.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1589">审核服务管道几乎是实时的，因此不能支持重复数据删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1589">The auditing service pipeline is near real time, and therefore can't support de-duplication.</span></span>
 
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1590">**Office 365 审核数据是否跨地域流动？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1590">**Does Office 365 auditing data flow across geographies?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1591">否。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1591">No.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1592">我们目前在 NA（北美）、EMEA（欧洲、中东和非洲）和 APAC（亚太地区）进行了审核管道部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1592">We currently have auditing pipeline deployments in the NA (North America), EMEA (Europe, Middle East, and Africa) and APAC (Asia Pacific) regions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1593">但是，我们可能会跨这些区域流动数据以实现负载平衡，并且仅在现场出现问题时才会这样做。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1593">However, we may flow the data across these regions for load-balancing and only during live-site issues.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1594">当我们执行这些活动时，传输中的数据会被加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1594">When we do perform these activities, the data in transit is encrypted.</span></span>   
 
<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1595">**审核数据是否已加密？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1595">**Is auditing data encrypted?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3863b-1596">审核数据存储在部署审核管道的同一区域内的 Exchange 邮箱中（静态数据）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1596">Auditing data is stored in Exchange mailboxes (data at rest) in the same region where the auditing pipeline is deployed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1597">此数据未加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1597">This data is not encrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3863b-1598">但是，传输中的数据始终是加密的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3863b-1598">However, data in transit is always encrypted.</span></span>
